Grid is a program which makes it easy to add a gridded overlay onto an image. In other words, it squares up the image for you.\r\n\r\nSplitting an image up into sections, to help us draw it, is something humans have been doing for centuries. With the dawn of the twenty-first century, though, it seems we have let this technique stagnate. We are still drawing the grid by hand and that includes computers (line or pen tool anyone?). I am sure you agree when I say it is a good thing to teach children how to do by hand in their art class. But... it becomes tedious the more you do it and, once you know how to do it, there is very little to learn or improve upon. This is where Paint Grid comes in.\r\n\r\nTo use Paint Grid, drag and drop a .jpg or .png file into the preview area.
